Introduction

Base URL: http://localhost:8000

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

AppointmentRace

–ú–µ—Ç–æ–¥—ã –æ—Ç–≤–µ—á–∞—é—â–∏–µ –∑–∞ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤

toggle

requires authentication

–ó–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –∏ –æ—Ç–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞ –≥–æ–Ω–∫—É

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/2/toggle-appointment-race" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"surname\": \"molestiae\",
    \"patronymic\": \"veritatis\",
    \"dateOfBirth\": \"2025-03-19T07:13:42\",
    \"city\": \"assumenda\",
    \"region\": \"eius\",
    \"inn\": 18,
    \"snils\": \"sed\",
    \"phoneNumber\": 15,
    \"startNumber\": 14,
    \"group\": \"sed\",
    \"rank\": \"sapiente\",
    \"rankNumber\": \"et\",
    \"community\": \"quas\",
    \"coach\": \"nihil\",
    \"motoStamp\": \"commodi\",
    \"locationId\": \"unde\",
    \"gradeId\": \"et\",
    \"numberAndSeria\": \"quibusdam\",
    \"documentIds\": [
        17
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/2/toggle-appointment-race"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "surname": "molestiae",
    "patronymic": "veritatis",
    "dateOfBirth": "2025-03-19T07:13:42",
    "city": "assumenda",
    "region": "eius",
    "inn": 18,
    "snils": "sed",
    "phoneNumber": 15,
    "startNumber": 14,
    "group": "sed",
    "rank": "sapiente",
    "rankNumber": "et",
    "community": "quas",
    "coach": "nihil",
    "motoStamp": "commodi",
    "locationId": "unde",
    "gradeId": "et",
    "numberAndSeria": "quibusdam",
    "documentIds": [
        17
    ]
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
    "status": "success",
    "message": "messages.appointment_race.create.success"
}

Example response (404):


{
    "status": "error",
    "message": "messages.error.not_found"
}

Example response (404):


{
    "status": "error",
    "message": "messages.appointment.create.grade_not_exists"
}

Example response (409):


{
    "status": "error",
    "message": "messages.error.exists_appointment_race"
}

Example response (422):


{
    "status": "success",
    "message": "messages.appointment.create_table.many_documents",
    "documents": []
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/races/{id}/toggle-appointment-race

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

URL Parameters

id   integer   

The ID of the race. Example: 2

Body Parameters

surname   string   

Example: molestiae

patronymic   string   

Example: veritatis

dateOfBirth   string   

Must be a valid date. Example: 2025-03-19T07:13:42

city   string   

Example: assumenda

region   string  optional  

Example: eius

inn   integer   

Example: 18

snils   string   

Example: sed

phoneNumber   integer   

Example: 15

startNumber   integer   

Must be at least 1. Must not be greater than 999. Example: 14

group   string   

Example: sed

rank   string   

Example: sapiente

rankNumber   string  optional  

Example: et

community   string  optional  

Example: quas

coach   string  optional  

Example: nihil

motoStamp   string   

Example: commodi

locationId   string   

The id of an existing record in the locations table. Example: unde

gradeId   string   

The id of an existing record in the grades table. Example: et

commandId   string  optional  

The id of an existing record in the commands table.

numberAndSeria   string   

Example: quibusdam

documentIds   integer[]  optional

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/races/2/appointment-race/users" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"paginate\": false,
    \"page\": \"enim\",
    \"limit\": 23
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/2/appointment-race/users"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "paginate": false,
    "page": "enim",
    "limit": 23
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"ddmlfhmnzid\",
    \"desc\": \"cmsasyjj\",
    \"price\": 15079.3057688,
    \"trackId\": 10
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/attendances"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "ddmlfhmnzid",
    "desc": "cmsasyjj",
    "price": 15079.3057688,
    "trackId": 10
};

    headers,

}).then(response => response.json());

Register

–†–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ü–∏—è –Ω–æ–≤–æ–≥–æ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/register" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "name=gebpyzwqtil"\
    --form "email=lurline.borer@example.org"\
    --form "password=M=IWP_xNL"\
    --form "password_confirmation=enim"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/register"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('name', 'gebpyzwqtil');
body.append('email', 'lurline.borer@example.org');
body.append('password', 'M=IWP_xNL');
body.append('password_confirmation', 'enim');

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
    "status": "success",
    "message": "messages.auth.register.success",
    "access_token": "22|CeIyp5tZJbPXy6P7EzLZBCcgU0RR5LIDg9rkBSef97cc7654",
    "token_type": "Bearer",
    "user": {
        "id": 181,
        "name": "Desiree Kuhic",
        "email": "ila72@example.net",
        "email_verified_at": "2025-03-19T07:13:34.000000Z",

    }
}

    "http://localhost:8000/api/cups"

    "Content-Type": "application/json",

};

    "name": "kul",

    "stages": "uxmkigwkbedlyxhssnoymk",
    "locationId": 7
};

    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

    --form "number=molestias"\
    --form "issuedWhom=nobis"\
    --form "itWorksDate=a"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/users/cabinet/documents/1/update"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('number', 'molestias');
body.append('issuedWhom', 'nobis');
body.append('itWorksDate', 'a');

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example request:

    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \

    --form "gradeIds[]=3"\
    --form "locationId=13"\
    --form "statusId=7"\
    --form "cupIds[]=19"

    "http://localhost:8000/api/races"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('name', 'spasiplpobzbzgrkrayoofyeunkhgogkgunxkehrrpsvmgxxjmek');
body.append('desc', 'provident');
body.append('dateStart', '2025-03-19T07:13:39');
body.append('recordEnd', '2025-03-19T07:13:39');
body.append('trackId', '16');
body.append('images[]', '');
body.append('gradeIds[]', '3');
body.append('locationId', '13');
body.append('statusId', '7');
body.append('cupIds[]', '19');

    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());
